***переговорить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переговорить.html>переговори́ть</a> (13677)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переговорить.html>переговори́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregovorítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to talk, to have a talk, to speak <i>(to, with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переговорить.html>переговори́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peregovorítʹ</b> po telefónu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to talk on/by the telephone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переговорить.html>переговорю́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ja <b>peregovorjú</b> s nim ob étom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll speak to him about it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to discuss, to cover
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тем</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переговорить.html>переговори́ть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stólʹko tem, što i ne <b>peregovorítʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there are so many things to discuss you can't cover them all</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to talk down, to outtalk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переговорить.html>переговори́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>кого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:угодный.html>уго́дно</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>peregovorít</b> kovó ugódno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he can outtalk anyone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***перегон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегон.html>перего́н</a> (23756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнать.html>перегна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peregnátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,with the vocalism of the imperfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегонять.html>перегоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peregonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегон.html>перего́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегон.html>перего́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегон.html>перего́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегон.html>перего́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stage <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a journey</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>stretch, span <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a railway line, between stations</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>driving <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of animals</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***перегонять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегонять.html>перегоня́ть</a> (22666)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гонять.html>гоня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегонять.html>перегоня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregonjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегнать.html>перегна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive (somewhere else), to ferry</li>
<li>to distill</li>
<li>to surpass, to overtake</li>
<li>to outrun, to outdistance</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнать.html>гнать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gnatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегонять.html>перегоня́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregonjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rare</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to banish, to exile (many people)</li></ol>

***перегореть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегореть.html>перегоре́ть</a> (19815)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гореть.html>горе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gorétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегореть.html>перегоре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregorétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перегора́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to burn out <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a fire, fuse, bulb, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burn to ashes, to burn to nothing</li>
<li>to fade <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">also figuratively, of feelings, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<li>to block, to obstruct

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегружать.html>перегружа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregružátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузить.html>перегрузи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to overload, to surcharge</li>
<li>to overload, to overwork</li>
<li>to overburden</li>
<li>to transship, to transfer</li>
<li>to reboot, to reload, to restart</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузка.html>перегру́зка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peregrúzka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>гру<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ть</a></b>

Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузить.html>перегрузи́ть</a>.

***перегрузить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузить.html>перегрузи́ть</a> (16153)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грузить.html>грузи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gruzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузить.html>перегрузи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregruzítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегружать.html>перегружа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to overload, to surcharge</li>
<li>to overload, to overwork</li>
<li>to overburden</li>
<li>to transship, to transfer</li>
<li>to reboot, to reload, to restart</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузка.html>перегру́зка</a> (10351)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузить.html>перегрузи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peregruzítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузка.html>перегру́зка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peregrúzka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузка.html>перегру́зки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузка.html>перегру́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузка.html>перегру́зок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>overload, surcharge</li>
<li>overload, overwork</li>
<li>transfer, transshipment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перегрузка.html>перегру́зка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:баржа.html>баржи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>кора́бль</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>peregrúzka</b> s barži na koráblʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">transshipment from the lighter to the ship</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="разговорное">разг.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:протяжный.html>протя́жный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затихать.html>затиха́ющий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:усиливаться.html>уси́ливающийся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:низкий.html>ни́зкий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звук.html>звук</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:гул.html>гул</a>; гуденье <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:временный.html>вре́менными</a> затиханиями <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>Ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:успеть.html>успе́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промолвить.html>промо́лвить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:издалека.html>издалека́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:словно.html>сло́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гром.html>гром</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекат.html>перека́тами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:перегуд.html>перегу́дами</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ударить.html>уда́рил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страшный.html>стра́шный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:орудийный.html>оруди́йный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:залп.html>залп</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><a href="https://ru.wikipedia.org/wiki/%D0%93%D0%B0%D0%B9%D0%B4%D0%B0%D1%80,_%D0%90%D1%80%D0%BA%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%B9_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:Гайдар, Аркадий Петрович"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***перед.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> (15531)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">передъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*perdъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*per-</i>, whence also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перез</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perez</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пред.html>пред</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péred</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>in front of, before</li>
<li>right/immediately before</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The preposition takes nouns in the instrumental case.</li>
<li><b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span></b> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> have similar meanings, but they are not interchangeable.
<dl><dd>When speaking about time:
<dl><dd><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:момент.html>моме́нта</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do moménta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> can mean quite a long time, whereas <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:момент.html>моме́нтом</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><b>péred</b> moméntom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> means <b>just</b> before the very moment.</dd>
<dd>Examples:</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́тимся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ты</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Daváj vstrétimsja do rabóty.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let’s meet before work.</span></dd><dl><dd>(<span class="e-source">any time between now and when we start work, and the meeting could be anywhere</span>)</dd></dl></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встретиться.html>встре́тимся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́той</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Daváj vstrétimsja <b>péred</b> rabótoj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Let’s meet <b>before</b> work.</span></dd><dl><dd>(<span class="e-source">just before we start work, immediately before work, and probably at the job site</span>)</dd></dl></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd>When speaking about space:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>До</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>города́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:далеко.html>далеко́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Do gorodá ješčó dalekó.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The city is still far away.</span></dd><dl><dd>(<span class="e-source">measured from here to there</span>)</dd></dl></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дойти.html>дошёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перекресток.html>перекрёстка</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja došól do perekrjóstka</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I reached the crossroads.</span></dd><dl><dd>(<span class="e-source">going from here to there</span>)</dd></dl></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>сою́зом</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a>» <a href = vnd.unilang:ставиться.html>ста́вится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:запятая.html>запята́я</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Péred</b> sojúzom “što” stávitsja zapjatája.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A comma is placed <b>before</b> the conjunction “što”.</span></dd><dl><dd>(<span class="e-source">immediately before that word</span>)</dd></dl></dl></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>The preposition <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span></b> can be combined with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мым</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sámym</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. For example:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приготовиться.html>пригото́вились</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́менам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мым</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́дом</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">My prigotóvilisʹ k ekzámenam <b>péred</b> sámym obédom.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">We prepared for the exams <b>right before</b> lunch.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd>Sentences with <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мым</a></span></b> use perfective verbs. Compared to sentences with perfective verbs while using the ordinary <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span></b>, it has a much shorter interval between the completed action/event and the particular action/event that the <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мым</a></span></b> modifies. Hence, <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мым</a></span></b> has a bigger emphasis meaning-wise than the ordinary <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></span></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пред.html>пред</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pred</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предо.html>предо</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́ред</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">péred</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>пе́реда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>переда́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>передо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>front, forepart</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>пе́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ред</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>Предло́г</a>; неизменяемое <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>Употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> твор. п.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочетание.html>сочета́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> местоимением <i><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мной</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мно́ю</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>передо</a></i>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:передо.html>передо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мной</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>Обы́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:речевой.html>речево́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поток.html>пото́ке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сливаться.html>слива́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:последующий.html>после́дующим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́вом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:превращаться.html>превраща́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> клитику (<a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>стано́вится</a> безударным).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-перед-</b>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:напротив.html>напро́тив</a> чего-либо, <a href = vnd.unilang:спереди.html>спе́реди</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> какого-то <a href = vnd.unilang:объект.html>объе́кта</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́котором</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстояние.html>расстоя́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>Пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́мом</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><span class="citation-source"> </span></i></span></span></span> <span class="example-fullblock"><br><span class="example-block" style="color:darkgreen"><a href = vnd.unilang:перед.html>Пе́ред</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызов.html>вы́зовами</a>. <span class="example-details" style="font-size:smaller;"> <i><span class="citation-source"> </span></i></span></span></span></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> чего-либо:

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передавать.html>передава́ть</a> (2415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передавать.html>передава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hand over, to deliver, to give</li>
<li>to broadcast, to transmit</li>
<li>to reproduce, to render</li>
<li>to tell, to take a message</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ча</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredáča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передатчик.html>переда́тчик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredátčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передавать.html>передава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передаваться.html>передава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передаться.html>переда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go over to, to spread</li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 2b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:передаться.html>переда́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>пере-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-да-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ва</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>пере-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-да-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-т-чик</b>.

***передать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a> (924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">передати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*perdati</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*per-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dati</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предать.html>преда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передавать.html>передава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hand over, to deliver, to give</li>
<li>to broadcast, to transmit</li>
<li>to reproduce, to render</li>
<li>to tell, to take a message</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передавать.html>передава́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">peredavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***передаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передаться.html>переда́ться</a> (17428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передаться.html>переда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передаваться.html>передава́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go over to, to spread</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передать.html>переда́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">peredátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***передача.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ча</a> (2239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ча</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">peredáča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́чи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:передача.html>переда́ч</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>delivery</li>
<li>communication, handing over, passing, transfer, transmission</li>
<li>parcel</li>
<li>broadcast, broadcasting, relaying, telecast, transmission</li>
<li>gear, gearing, drive, transmission</li></ol>
